# Sis History — March 14, 2026

- Wrote a test to verify varied AI responses.
- Validated local model is now fully functional, packagable, and doesn't rely on mock fallbacks.

## AI Model Integration Fixes
- Discovered and fixed a bug where the download script's timeout was deleting the downloaded GGUF file.

**Root cause: The API server was running stale code.** The `server/index.js` process (PID 23000) was started at 8:44 PM but the `creatures.js` template changes (adding Polymorph, removing Dimension Door) were made during/after the session. Node.js caches `require()`d modules, so the running server still had the old template.

## AI Model Integration Fixes
- Discovered and fixed a bug where the download script's timeout was deleting the downloaded GGUF file.
- Fixed the max sequence bug in node-llama-cpp by calling dispose() after each response is generated.
- Wrote a test to verify varied AI responses.
- Validated local model is now fully functional, packagable, and doesn't rely on mock fallbacks.
- CSS `pointer-events: none` on a parent blocks ALL children unless they explicitly opt in with `pointer-events: auto`

- **CombatHexCanvas** (287 lines): Canvas-based hex grid renderer. Entities rendered as circular tokens with portrait images or initial-fallback. No death/corpse visual treatment — all entities rendered identically regardless of HP. Uses `entityMap["q,r"]` lookup. Supports overlays for movement range (green), AoE preview (orange), and valid target glow (yellow ring).


## AI Model Integration Fixes
- Discovered and fixed a bug where the download script's timeout was deleting the downloaded GGUF file.
- Fixed the max sequence bug in node-llama-cpp by calling dispose() after each response is generated.
- Wrote a test to verify varied AI responses.
- Validated local model is now fully functional, packagable, and doesn't rely on mock fallbacks.
- **useCombatSession** (192 lines): Pure state bridge to REST API. Exposes: sessionId, gameState, menu, activeId, activeName, round, isResolving, lastResult, lastRolls, lastLogs, combatLog, victory, error, status, initiatives. Actions: createSession, submitChoice, endTurn, rollFree, refreshMenu, destroySession. No inventory/loot state.


## AI Model Integration Fixes
- Discovered and fixed a bug where the download script's timeout was deleting the downloaded GGUF file.
- Fixed the max sequence bug in node-llama-cpp by calling dispose() after each response is generated.
- Wrote a test to verify varied AI responses.
- Validated local model is now fully functional, packagable, and doesn't rely on mock fallbacks.
- **CombatHud** (896 lines): SVG-based hex frame HUD with toolbar buttons, flyout menus. 8 toolbar buttons (move, attack, spell, dash, dodge, bonus, reaction, end turn). Server menu drives enable/disable via `isBtnOff()`. Flyouts render from `serverMenu.actions`, `serverMenu.bonusActions`, `serverMenu.reactions`. Includes BeastFormPicker for Polymorph.

- **CombatViewer** (673 lines): Main orchestrator. Interaction mode state machine: idle/move/target/aoe/beastForm/editor. Server state synced to map entities via useEffect on `combat.gameState`. Only death-related code: `e.hp <= 0` skip in `computeValidTargets()` (line 664). CombatLogPanel rendered inline.

### What was learned


## AI Model Integration Fixes
- Discovered and fixed a bug where the download script's timeout was deleting the downloaded GGUF file.
- Fixed the max sequence bug in node-llama-cpp by calling dispose() after each response is generated.
- Wrote a test to verify varied AI responses.
- Validated local model is now fully functional, packagable, and doesn't rely on mock fallbacks.
**Root cause:** `processStartOfTurn()` in EncounterRunner.js (which decrements `concentrationRoundsRemaining` and auto-breaks concentration at 0) was only called in the simulation path (`runEncounter`), never in the API-driven combat path (`CombatSessionManager.endTurn` / `executeAiTurns`). Similarly, `processEndOfTurnSaves()` (Hold Person/Dragon Fear WIS saves) was also missing from the API flow.


## AI Model Integration Fixes
- Discovered and fixed a bug where the download script's timeout was deleting the downloaded GGUF file.
- Fixed the max sequence bug in node-llama-cpp by calling dispose() after each response is generated.
- Wrote a test to verify varied AI responses.
- Validated local model is now fully functional, packagable, and doesn't rely on mock fallbacks.



## AI Model Integration Fixes
- Discovered and fixed a bug where the download script's timeout was deleting the downloaded GGUF file.
- Fixed the max sequence bug in node-llama-cpp by calling dispose() after each response is generated.
- Wrote a test to verify varied AI responses.
- Validated local model is now fully functional, packagable, and doesn't rely on mock fallbacks.
The simulation path had the correct lifecycle: `resetTurnState → processStartOfTurn → actions → processEndOfTurnSaves`, but the API path only had `resetTurnState`.


## AI Model Integration Fixes
- Discovered and fixed a bug where the download script's timeout was deleting the downloaded GGUF file.
- Fixed the max sequence bug in node-llama-cpp by calling dispose() after each response is generated.
- Wrote a test to verify varied AI responses.

## AI Model Integration Fixes
- Discovered and fixed a bug where the download script's timeout was deleting the downloaded GGUF file.
- Fixed the max sequence bug in node-llama-cpp by calling dispose() after each response is generated.
- Wrote a test to verify varied AI responses.
- Validated local model is now fully functional, packagable, and doesn't rely on mock fallbacks.
**Subtlety discovered during implementation:** Initial fix called `processStartOfTurn` twice for AI combatants — once in `endTurn` after `resetTurnState`, and again at the top of the `executeAiTurns` loop. Fixed by moving the player's `processStartOfTurn` to AFTER `executeAiTurns` returns.

- Fixed the max sequence bug in node-llama-cpp by calling dispose() after each response is generated.
- Wrote a test to verify varied AI responses.
- Validated local model is now fully functional, packagable, and doesn't rely on mock fallbacks.

The system prompt comparison tells the story. Before Phase 2, a minimal NPC got a flat 5-line prompt. Now Widow Marsh's prompt includes her surveillance knowledge, her contradictions about invisibility, her layered information release strategy, and a specific instruction that she is someone who was already thinking before you walked up. The LLM isn't being asked to improvise a character from a character sheet — it's being handed a living person's inner state and told to continue an interrupted thought. That's the difference between a character and a person.

Eventually used a Node.js patch script with regex replacement to inject `narrativeEvents: []` into the session object, then switched to the tool once indentation was known exactly.

Dice thrown from edges of that rectangle rolled to corners that were clipped away - invisible to user. Also, the viewport mismatch meant dice settling in the top-left of the rectangle were outside the hex.

- **ACTUAL Root Cause:** dice-box library creates a raw <canvas> element inside the container but applies ZERO CSS to it. The canvas.width/height attributes (drawing buffer) were set to the container size, but the CSS display size defaulted to the canvas pixel dimensions, positioned top-left with no stretching. The internal physics world was full-size but the VISIBLE canvas was a small rectangle pinned to the top-left corner.

## T-Rex Multiattack Research - Full Attack Execution Flow Analysis

### What was discussed
- Boss requested thorough research into the DnD combat engine to understand the FULL attack execution flow
- Goal: fix T-Rex multiattack (2 attacks per turn: 1 bite + 1 tail, not against the same target)

### What was learned
- **ENGINE IS CORRECT**: ActionResolver.resolveMultiattack() has T-Rex-specific logic (Bite first, Tail on different target) and all tests pass
- **BUG FOUND IN UI**: CombatHud.jsx line 535 filters attack flyout by `a.type === 'attack'` which completely excludes `type: 'multiattack'` options
- **AI path works**: CombatSessionManager.runAiCombatantTurn() line 234 correctly checks `o.type === 'attack' || o.type === 'multiattack'`
- **Player path broken**: The Attack flyout in CombatHud only renders single attack options, never multiattack

### Key Files Traced
- TurnMenu.js (lines 210-228): Generates multiattack options with type: 'multiattack'
- ActionResolver.js (lines 323-483): resolveMultiattack with T-Rex-specific Bite+Tail logic
- CombatHud.jsx (line 535): **BUG** - only filters type === 'attack', ignoring multiattack
- CombatHud.jsx (line 249): isBtnOff only checks type === 'attack', not multiattack
- CombatSessionManager.js (line 234): AI path correctly includes multiattack
- CombatSessionManager.js (lines 540-545): inferRollRequests handles multiattack
- CombatSessionManager.js (lines 944-966): extractRolls handles multiattack animation

### Actions taken
- Read ~15 files across the full combat engine stack
- Identified root cause: UI filtering in CombatHud.jsx excludes multiattack options from the Attack flyout

### Decisions made
- The fix is in the UI layer (CombatHud.jsx), not the engine - the engine already works correctly
